# Dialogue Index (2369 conversations, organized by mission/task)

Main story (01) uses level→journal reference chains. Side content (02–10) is
organized to per-task folders via the algorithm in
`reverse-engineering/reorg_sidequests.py` (game level→conversation references +
journal titles). Folders prefixed `_` are region/category buckets where no single
task could be resolved.
